<userid>113335216233021176387<//userid>< Name>
Dave Neely< /Name>
< Date>
1522422973088<//Date>
<Rating>4< /Rating>< review>
I ordered delivery from this restaurant while staying at a SF hotel. The delivery was made in decent time and I enjoyed the food. I ordered spring rolls, green onion pancakes, chicken fried rice and vegetable & dumpling soup. The spring rolls were good, the cabbage pieces inside were plentiful but chopped a bit large for my taste (they would pull out of the roll when you took a bite). But the flavors were good so that wasn't a big deal. The green onion pancake was ok if a bit greasy. The fried rice was very good, I liked the flavors they came up with for it. They didn't have my favorite wonton soup but they had something called vegetable and dumpling soup which was pretty good. There was a lot of bok choy in a chicken broth, and the dumplings were decent. They didn't seem hand made but they were still good. All in all I was pleased with my order and I would order from them again.<//review>

113145556773027671117</user>
<Time>1528683151652</Time><Gmap_id>0x808580846c862551:0x4177fad2c2fed957<//Gmap_id>< review>
For me, this is the quintessential take-out restaurant. While there are dine-in options and rarely some folks doing just that, it is really not much to look at inside.

We only ever get the traditional Szechuan dish, spicy boiled fish, or 'shui zhu yu'. It is not the best we've ever had, but it is up there. Nicely spiced, a little disappointing on the 'numbing' from the sichuan peppercorns - but made up for in taste, quality of the fish, and a good portion size.

The people that run the place are lovely and accommodating.< /review>

To think, I had lived next to a mecca of delicious spicy Chinese food. Maybe I just ordered the wrong items? But here's what I got.
Pork Belly with Garlic and Spice: 0/5. I had expected those lovely tender chunks of pork belly glazed with garlic and spice. YUM. What I got was a soup that was mildly spicy at best with cold, unappetizing thin and chewy pieces. None of the sauce was picked up either - it was very bland.
Kung Pao: 2/5. Whoever wrote this would be so spicy they sweated does not ever do sichuan or Indian. I specifically asked for spicy (two times - once in writing and once by checking "spicy") in the request for delivery. It was bland.
String Beans: 3/5 - Probably the best of the dishes. Dried and pretty spicy.

<name>Stephanie Hardman</name><date>1408467081202<//date><Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
I love this hometown, cozy restaurant cafe. The style here is an organically-grown, family-owned and operated LOCALS joint with the flair of a staycation. While your butt is cradled in the comfy chairs one can enjoy any number of delicious drinks. Lime in the Coconut is hands down my favorite drink right now. It has the right amount of sweetness accompanying the tart and creamy flavor of the fruity components.

Food wise, this place has you covered! Hawaiian plates and salads are always fresh and crafted with love. I never feel rushed or get the sense that the people working here consider this a "job".. maybe its the reggae! I definitely feel a sense of community and leisure when I lounge here sipping a tea or dirty chai.< /review>

The smog station starts at 9 am. I don't have a google account, so I'm posting with my wife's, but I have taken my RV and my truck here and the guy is quick, efficient, and professional. I gave four stars as I've paid less for smogs in the past, but not knowing what the going rate is, perhaps that's unfair.<//text>
